I am a doctoral student in computer vision and will graduate next year. My career plan is to become a teacher in a university, so after graduating with my doctorate, I plan to find a professor who is engaged in the same research field to conduct postdoctoral work. ```json output_result
# About Me

## Research Areas
**Main Research Area:** Visual Generative Models

**Specific Fields:** Application and innovation of diffusion models, flow matching and related technologies in tasks such as image generation, video generation, and cross-modal generation.

## Research Interests

My research focuses on advancing the frontier of visual content generation through deep generative models. I am particularly interested in:

- **Diffusion Models & Flow Matching**: Developing efficient sampling strategies and improving the quality-diversity trade-off in generative processes
- **Video Generation**: Exploring temporal consistency and motion dynamics in video synthesis using state-of-the-art generative frameworks
- **Cross-modal Generation**: Bridging different modalities (text-to-image, image-to-video, audio-visual synthesis) through unified generative architectures
- **Controllable Generation**: Investigating methods for fine-grained control over generated content while maintaining high fidelity
- **Efficient Inference**: Optimizing generative models for real-world deployment with reduced computational costs

## News

üîç **I am actively seeking a postdoctoral position at a university in Hong Kong.** If you are interested in collaboration or have opportunities available, please feel free to contact me.

üìß Contact: [tadaawc@adp.com]

## Recent Publications

Please refer to my google scholar page for this part!

## Education

- Ph.D. in CSE, ABU, 2026 (expected)
- M.S. in CSE, ABU, 2021
- B.S. in EE, BCU, 2019

## Selected Projects

### Project 1: Diffusion Models for High-Quality Image Synthesis
Developed an advanced diffusion-based framework that significantly improves the fidelity and resolution of generated images. Introduced novel architectural enhancements and sampling techniques to achieve state-of-the-art results on benchmark datasets.

### Project 2: Consistent Video Generation via Flow Matching
Proposed a flow matching approach for temporal-consistent video generation, enabling the synthesis of realistic motion and persistent object appearances across frames. The method achieves robust performance in both unconditional and conditional video generation tasks.

### Project 3: Cross-Modal Generative Framework
Designed a unified generative model capable of handling multiple modalities, such as text-to-image and image-to-video generation. The framework supports smooth cross-modal translation and demonstrates strong results on several public datasets.

---

*Feel free to reach out for research collaboration, academic discussions, or potential opportunities!*
```

class=\"blog-post \">\r\n                <div class=\"container\">\r\n            <div class=\"row\">\r\n                <div class=\"col-sm-9 blog-post--sidebar\">\r\n                    <div class=\"blog-post__title\">\r\n    <h1 class=\"h2\">Paper Digest: CVPR 2025 Papers &#038; Highlights</h1>    <div class=\"blog-post__title-meta\">\r\n        <span><span class=\"posted-on\"><span class=\"ion-ios-clock-outline\"></span> <time class=\"entry-date published\" datetime=\"2025-06-07T00:00:00-04:00\">June 7, 2025</time><time class=\"updated\" datetime=\"2025-06-09T12:52:11-04:00\">June 9, 2025</time></span><span class=\"byline\"> </span></span>\r\n        <span><span class=\"author vcard\"><span class=\"ion-ios-person\"></span> <a class=\"url fn n\" href=\"https://www.paperdigest.org/author/admin/\">admin</a></span></span>\r\n    </div>\r\n</div>                    <div class=\"blog-post__content\">\r\n                        <p><body> The IEEE Conference on Computer Vision and Pattern Recognition (CVPR) is one of the top computer vision conferences in the world. To help the community quickly catch up on the work presented in this conference, Paper Digest Team processed all accepted papers, and generated one highlight sentence (typically the main topic) for each paper. Readers are encouraged to read these machine generated highlights to quickly get the main idea of each paper.</p>\n<p>Note: CVPR-2025 accepts more than 2,800 papers, this page only includes 500 of them selected by our daily paper digest algorithm. Interested users can choose to read <a href=\"https://www.paperdigest.org/digest/?topic=cvpr&#038;year=2025\">All 2,800 CVPR-2025 papers</a> in a separate page.</p>\n<p> To search for papers presented at CVPR-2025 on a specific topic, please make use of the <a href =\"https://www.paperdigest.org/digest/?type=search&#038;topic=cvpr&#038;year=2025\">search by venue (CVPR-2025)</a> service. To summarize the latest research published at CVPR-2025 on a specific topic, you can utilize the <a href =\"https://www.paperdigest.org/digest/?type=review&#038;topic=cvpr&#038;year=2025\">review by venue (CVPR-2025)</a> service. If you are interested in browsing papers by author, we have a comprehensive list of <a target=\"_blank\" href='https://www.paperdigest.org/digest/?type=authors&#038;topic=cvpr&#038;year=2025' rel=\"noopener\">~ 12,000 authors (CVPR-2025)</a>. Additionally, you may want to explore our <a href='https://resources.paperdigest.org/2025/03/most-influential-cvpr-papers-2025-03-version/'>&#8220;Best Paper&#8221; Digest (CVPR)</a>, which lists the most influential CVPR papers since 1988.</p>\n<p>We&#8217;ve developed a service &#8211; <a href=\"https://www.paperdigest.org/research/?topic=cvpr&#038;year=2025\">CVPR-2025 Research Report</a> that synthesizes the latest findings from CVPR 2025 into comprehensive reports. For instance, we&#8217;ve generated sample reports on <a href=\"https://www.paperdigest.org/report/?id=advances-in-3d-from-multi-view-and-sensors-insights-from-cvpr-2025-papers\">Advances in 3D from Multi-View and Sensors: Insights from CVPR 2025 Papers</a> and <a href=\"https://www.paperdigest.org/report/?id=advances-in-image-and-video-synthesis-insights-from-cvpr-2025-papers\">Advances in Image and Video Synthesis: Insights from CVPR 2025 Papers</a>. We encourage interested users to utilize our service to create tailored reports on other emerging topics.</p>\n<p>This curated list is created by the Paper Digest Team. Experience the cutting-edge capabilities of Paper Digest, an innovative AI-powered research platform that gets you the personalized and comprehensive updates on the latest research in your field. It also empowers you to <a href=\"https://www.paperdigest.org/reader\">read articles</a>, <a href=\"https://www.paperdigest.org/writer\">write articles</a>, <a href=\"https://www.paperdigest.org/copilot\">get answers</a>, <a href=\"https://www.paperdigest.org/review\">conduct literature reviews</a> and <a href=\"https://www.paperdigest.org/research\">generate research reports</a>.</p>\n<p>Experience the full potential of our services today!</p>\n<h4>TABLE 1: Paper Digest: CVPR 2025 Papers &#038; class=\"blog-post \">\r\n                <div class=\"container\">\r\n            <div class=\"row\">\r\n                <div class=\"col-sm-9 blog-post--sidebar\">\r\n                    <div class=\"blog-post__title\">\r\n    <h1 class=\"h2\">Most Influential CVPR Papers (2025-09 Version)</h1>    <div class=\"blog-post__title-meta\">\r\n        <span><span class=\"posted-on\"><span class=\"ion-ios-clock-outline\"></span> <time class=\"entry-date published\" datetime=\"2025-09-21T00:00:37-04:00\">September 21, 2025</time><time class=\"updated\" datetime=\"2025-09-22T14:45:27-04:00\">September 22, 2025</time></span><span class=\"byline\"> </span></span>\r\n        <span><span class=\"author vcard\"><span class=\"ion-ios-person\"></span> <a class=\"url fn n\" href=\"https://www.paperdigest.org/author/admin/\">admin</a></span></span>\r\n    </div>\r\n</div>                    <div class=\"blog-post__content\">\r\n                        <p><body> The IEEE Conference on Computer Vision and Pattern Recognition (CVPR) is one of the top computer vision conferences in the world. Paper Digest Team analyzes all papers published on CVPR in the past years, and presents the 15 most influential papers for each year. This ranking list is automatically constructed based upon citations from both research papers and granted patents, and will be frequently updated to reflect the most recent changes. To find the <u>latest version</u> of this list or the most influential papers from <u>other conferences/journals</u>, please visit <a href='https://www.paperdigest.org/best-paper-digest'>Best Paper Digest</a> page.  Note: the most influential papers may or may not include the papers that won the best paper awards. <b>(Version: 2025-09)</b></p>\n<p>To search or review papers within CVPR related to a specific topic, please use the <a href =\"https://www.paperdigest.org/digest/?type=search&#038;topic=cvpr\">search by venue (CVPR)</a> and <a href =\"https://www.paperdigest.org/digest/?type=review&#038;topic=cvpr\">review by venue (CVPR)</a> services. To browse the most productive CVPR authors by year ranked by #papers accepted, here are the <a target=\"_blank\" href='https://www.paperdigest.org/digest/?type=authors&#038;topic=cvpr&#038;year=2023' rel=\"noopener\">most productive CVPR authors</a> grouped by year. </p>\n<p>This list is created by the Paper Digest Team. Experience the cutting-edge capabilities of Paper Digest, an innovative AI-powered research platform that empowers you to <a href=\"https://www.paperdigest.org/reader\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">read articles</a>, <a href=\"https://www.paperdigest.org/writer\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">write articles</a>, <a href=\"https://www.paperdigest.org/copilot\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">get answers</a>, <a href=\"https://www.paperdigest.org/review\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">conduct literature reviews</a> and <a href=\"https://www.paperdigest.org/research\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">generate research reports</a>.</p>\n<p> Paper Digest Team<br /> New York City, New York, 10017<br /> team@paperdigest.org</p>\n<h4>TABLE 1: Most Influential CVPR Papers (2025-09 Version)</h4>\n<table>\n<col width=\"5%\"/>\n<col width=\"5%\"/>\n<col width=\"65%\"/>\n<col statistics</figcaption></figure><p style=\"font-size:15px;\"><big><b>How to interpret the columns above:</b></big><br><small>- <b>Count:</b> The total number of submissions is calculated as: <code>#Total = #Accept + #Reject + #Withdraw + #Desk Reject - #Post Decision Withdraw</code> (when applicable).</small><br><small>- <b>Rates:</b> Each status rate is computed as <code>#Status Occurrence / #Total</code>, where the status can be Accept, Reject, etc. For example, if there are 100 total submissions and 27 were accepted, the <code>Accept Rate = 27 / 100 = 27%</code>.</small><br><small>- <b>min / max / mean / std:</b> These are statistical summaries of the <i>reviewer average scores per submission</i> within each decision tier (e.g., Accept tier). For example, if a paper received ratings of 3, 4, and 5, its average score is 4 ‚Äî and this average is used in the distribution. Suppose the Accept tier contains submissions with reviewer averages: {4.0, 3.1, 3.6}. Then, the <code>min = 3.1</code>, <code>max = 4.0</code>, <code>mean ‚âà 3.57</code>, and <code>std ‚âà 0.37</code>. If rating scores are publicly available, the statistics are based on submissions that opted in for release. If scores are collected from the community via the Google Form, the statistics reflect only those samples. When both community-collected and officially released scores are available, only the official scores are used for the displayed statistics.</small><br><small>- <b>Reject:</b> Refers only to submissions that opted in for public release. Please note that the number of opt-in records may be smaller than the actual number of rejections.</small><br><small>- <b>Withdraw:</b> Includes papers withdrawn by the authors, including those withdrawn after acceptance. Post-decision withdrawals are specifically marked as such.</small></p><br><p style=\"font-size:15px;\"><big><b>How to use the paper list below:</b></big><br><small>- <b>Overview:</b> This table presents papers from the <code>CVPR</code> conference, year <code>2025</code>.</small><br><small>- <b>Filtering:</b> By default, the table loads the first <code>100 records</code>. You can use the <code>filter box under each column header</code> to search within these loaded entries. Each column displays a <code>‚ÄúPer Column Match #‚Äù</code> to indicate how many results match that column‚Äôs filter. If you apply filters across multiple columns, the combined match count appears under <code>‚ÄúAll Filter Matches‚Äù</code>. To search the entire venue, click <code>‚ÄúClick to Fetch All‚Äù</code>. Note: on large venues, this may temporarily freeze your browser. Enabling <code>‚ÄúHide Rejected‚Äù</code> helps reduce loading time.</small><br><small>- <b>Sorting:</b> Click the <code>\"‚¨ç A‚ÄìZ\"</code> icon in a column header to <code>sort</code> the table. When a custom sort is applied, a new column <code>‚ÄúRow Index (R#)‚Äù</code> appears to reflect the updated order. The original default order ‚Äî based on <code>review rating</code>, then <code>review confidence</code>, then <code>title</code> ‚Äî is preserved in the <i>‚Äú#‚Äù</i> column. If any key is missing, fallback to the next priority field is applied.</small><br><small>- <b>Source Data:</b> Raw data is available on <a href=\"https://github.com/papercopilot/paperlists\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">GitHub</a> ‚Äî we welcome <code>stars</code> and <a href=\"https://github.com/papercopilot/paperlists/issues\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">issue reports</a> to help us improve the platform.</small></p><figure class=\"wp-block-table is-style-stripes\" style=\"font-size:15px\"><table id=\"paperlist\"><thead><tr class=\"filter-info\"><th colspan=\"9\" class=\"wp-element-caption\">Click for <a target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\" href=\"/statistics/CVPR-statistics/\">ALL available CVPR</a> statistics</figcaption></figure><p style=\"font-size:15px;\"><big><b>How to interpret the columns above:</b></big><br><small>- <b>Count:</b> The total number of submissions is calculated as: <code>#Total = #Accept + #Reject + #Withdraw + #Desk Reject - #Post Decision Withdraw</code> (when applicable).</small><br><small>- <b>Rates:</b> Each status rate is computed as <code>#Status Occurrence / #Total</code>, where the status can be Accept, Reject, etc. For example, if there are 100 total submissions and 27 were accepted, the <code>Accept Rate = 27 / 100 = 27%</code>.</small><br><small>- <b>min / max / mean / std:</b> These are statistical summaries of the <i>reviewer average scores per submission</i> within each decision tier (e.g., Accept tier). For example, if a paper received ratings of 3, 4, and 5, its average score is 4 ‚Äî and this average is used in the distribution. Suppose the Accept tier contains submissions with reviewer averages: {4.0, 3.1, 3.6}. Then, the <code>min = 3.1</code>, <code>max = 4.0</code>, <code>mean ‚âà 3.57</code>, and <code>std ‚âà 0.37</code>. If rating scores are publicly available, the statistics are based on submissions that opted in for release. If scores are collected from the community via the Google Form, the statistics reflect only those samples. When both community-collected and officially released scores are available, only the official scores are used for the displayed statistics.</small><br><small>- <b>Reject:</b> Refers only to submissions that opted in for public release. Please note that the number of opt-in records may be smaller than the actual number of rejections.</small><br><small>- <b>Withdraw:</b> Includes papers withdrawn by the authors, including those withdrawn after acceptance. Post-decision withdrawals are specifically marked as such.</small></p><br><p style=\"font-size:15px;\"><big><b>More about the chart above:</b></big><br><small><b>Author Matching Limitation:</b> When an author‚Äôs ID is not available, the system falls back to matching based on <b>alphabetical name string</b>. As a result, charts involving author counts (e.g., top authors, affiliations) may contain <b>redundant entries</b> if multiple authors share the same name.</small><br></p><br><p style=\"font-size:15px;\"><big><b>How to use the paper list below:</b></big><br><small>- <b>Overview:</b> This table presents papers from the <code>CVPR</code> conference, year <code>2025</code>.</small><br><small>- <b>Filtering:</b> By default, the table loads the first <code>100 records</code>. You can use the <code>filter box under each column header</code> to search within these loaded entries. Each column displays a <code>‚ÄúPer Column Match #‚Äù</code> to indicate how many results match that column‚Äôs filter. If you apply filters across multiple columns, the combined match count appears under <code>‚ÄúAll Filter Matches‚Äù</code>. To search the entire venue, click <code>‚ÄúClick to Fetch All‚Äù</code>. Note: on large venues, this may temporarily freeze your browser. Enabling <code>‚ÄúHide Rejected‚Äù</code> helps reduce loading time.</small><br><small>- <b>Sorting:</b> Click the <code>\"‚¨ç A‚ÄìZ\"</code> icon in a column header to <code>sort</code> the table. When a custom sort is applied, a new column <code>‚ÄúRow Index (R#)‚Äù</code> appears to reflect the updated order. The original default order ‚Äî based on <code>review rating</code>, then <code>review confidence</code>, then <code>title</code> ‚Äî is preserved in the <i>‚Äú#‚Äù</i> column. If any key is missing, fallback to the next priority field is applied.</small><br><small>- <b>Hover & Linking:</b> <code>Author, affiliation, and country fields</code> are automatically linked. Hovering over an <code>author</code> highlights their affiliated organization and country, and vice versa. A mini profile card will also appear showing the author‚Äôs name and a gender-colored tag: <code>blue</code> for male, <code>pink</code> for female (white when unavailable). <code>Affiliation</code> metadata may take time to appear, as it‚Äôs parsed from the original publication. A dropdown lets you toggle between display formats. All names are normalized (e.g., official name, department, campus, abbreviations). The entire mapping is powered by an LLM backend. Country names follow <a href=\"https://unstats.un.org/unsd/methodology/m49/\" target=\"_blank\">United Nations naming conventions</a> and will be revised when needed <a href=\"https://papercopilot.com/contact-us/\" target=\"_blank\">on request</a> to prevent confusion.</small><br><small>- <b>Metrics:</b> Each paper includes a metrics column showing the review score and citation count from Google Scholar. If available, the citation count links to the corresponding Google Scholar profile. A value of <code>-1 or -</code> means the record was not found. Citations are updated periodically, not in real time.</small><br><small>- <b>Source Data:</b> Raw data is available on <a href=\"https://github.com/papercopilot/paperlists\" target=\"_blank\">GitHub</a> ‚Äî we welcome <code>stars</code> and <a href=\"https://github.com/papercopilot/paperlists/issues\" target=\"_blank\">issue reports</a> to help us improve the platform.</small></p><style>\n            .highlight {\n            background-color: #fffa9c !important;\n            font-weight: bold;\n            }\n            #author-popup a {\n            color: #0645ad;\n            text-decoration: none;\n            }\n            #author-popup a:hover {\n            text-decoration: underline;\n            }\n            </style><figure Return input if not a string\n      }\n    \n      const exceptions = ['and', 'of', 'on', 'the'];\n      const exceptions_uppercase = ['ieee', 'acm'];\n      const words = str.toLowerCase().split(' ');\n    \n      const titleCasedWords = words.map(word => {\n        if (exceptions.includes(word)) {\n          return word;\n        } \n        else if (exceptions_uppercase.includes(word)) {\n          return word.toUpperCase();\n        }\n        else {\n          return word.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + word.slice(1);\n        }\n      });\n    \n      return titleCasedWords.join(' ');\n '\\n');\n        \n            // Convert headers\n            markdown = markdown.replace(/###### (.*)/g, '<h6>$1</h6>');\n            markdown = markdown.replace(/##### (.*)/g, '<h5>$1</h5>');\n            markdown = markdown.replace(/#### (.*)/g, '<h5>$1</h5>');\n            markdown = markdown.replace(/### (.*)/g, '<h5>$1</h5>');\n            markdown = markdown.replace(/## (.*)/g, '<h4>$1</h4>');\n            markdown = markdown.replace(/# (.*)/g, '<h4>$1</h4>');\n\n            // Convert bold and italic\n            markdown = markdown.replace(/\\*\\*(.*?)\\*\\*/g, '<strong>$1</strong>');\n            markdown = markdown.replace(/\\*(.*?)\\*/g, '<em>$1</em>');\n\n            // Convert links\n            markdown = markdown.replace(/\\[(.*?)\\]\\((.*?)\\)/g, '<a href=\"$2\">$1</a>');\n\n            // Convert line breaks\n            markdown = markdown.replace(/\\n/g, '<br>');\n\n            return markdown;\n    }\n    \n\t\t\n    function extractPDUrl(text) {\n        const abcRegex = /https:\\/\\/www\\.paperdigest\\.org\\/(paper|patent|trial|grant|trademark|)\\/[^\\s\"]*/i; // Matches paper or patent URLs\n        const abcMatch = text.match(abcRegex);\n        if (abcMatch) {\n            return abcMatch[0].replace(/\"$/, \"\"); // Return the ABC URL if found\n        }\n        return ''; // Return null if no URL is found at all\n    }\n    \n    \n    function getPartBeforeSpace(str) {\n      if (str.includes(' ')) {\n        return str.substring(0, str.indexOf(' '));\n      } else {\n        return str;\n      }\n    }\n    \n    \n\tfunction copy_result() {\n        var result='';\n\t    if (related_work.innerText) {\n\t        var str= related_work.innerText.trim();\n            if (str) {\n              const ```json output_result
/**
 * üìù Paper List Filtering & AJAX Loader
 * ------------------------------------------------------------
 * This script powers the interactive conference paper list interface.
 * It supports dynamic loading, filtering, sorting, and highlighting 
 * of large-scale academic paper records using jQuery and AJAX.
 *
 * üîß Features & Responsibilities:
 *
 *  ‚úÖ Lazy Loads Papers via AJAX
 *     - `loadMoreRows()` fetches paginated rows and appends to the DOM.
 *     - Supports on-demand (`Load More`) and full preloading (`Fetch All`).
 *
 *  ‚úÖ Column-Based Filtering with Debounce
 *     - `applyFilters()` filters papers based on header input fields.
 *     - Rejection/withdrawn papers can be toggled via a dedicated button.
 *     - Filter application is debounced using `requestAnimationFrame()` + timeout.
 *
 *  ‚úÖ Rejection Status Caching
 *     - `cacheStatusData()` stores paper status in `data()` to minimize DOM access.
 *
 *  ‚úÖ Live Match Count & Hidden Row Tracking
 *     - Displays real-time filter matches per column.
 *     - Shows total visible vs. hidden (rejected/withdrawn) paper rows.
 *
 *  ‚úÖ Sorting Support
 *     - Clickable headers using `.sort-btn` allow toggling A-Z / Z-A sorting.
 *     - Sorts numerically or alphabetically based on column content.
 *     - Automatically updates row indices post-sort.
 *
 *  ‚úÖ Dynamic Column Visibility
 *     - `autotoggleEmptyColumns()` hides empty columns to improve readability.
 *     - Handles merged headers via `colspan`.
 *
 *  ‚úÖ Country-Aware Hover Highlighting
 *     - Highlights author/affiliation/country cells by shared country.
 *     - Country ‚Üí color mapping via fixed palette or dynamic pastel assignment.
 *
 *  ‚úÖ Author Info Popups
 *     - Hovering an `.author-link` shows floating div with linked profile (GS, homepage, DBLP, OpenReview).
 *     - Includes fade-in/out handling and flicker prevention.
 *
 *  ‚úÖ Affiliation Display Toggle
 *     - Switch between normalized name / department / abbreviation views via dropdown.
 *
 *  ‚úÖ Metrics Display Toggle
 *     - Dynamically change `.metrics-cell` display based on selected metric dimension.
 *
 * üèÅ Initialization Steps:
 *     1. Determine status column index (`findStatusColumnIndex()`).
 *     2. Load initial paper rows via `loadMoreRows()`.
 *     3. Attach filter inputs, sorting, and hover events.
 *     4. Cache initial row metadata and status.
 *
 * üí° Notes:
 *  - Table rows are not removed but hidden using `display: none` for stable layout.
 *  - Designed for high scalability: tested on large datasets (10k+ entries).
 *  - Compatible with WordPress AJAX (`ajaxmeta.ajax_url`) and dynamic DOM extensions.
 */

jQuery(document).ready(function ($) {
  var batch = 0;
  var n_records = 0;
  var container = $('#paperlist');
  var is_fetchall = false;
  var is_hide_reject = false;
  var hiddenCount = 0;
  var filterTimeout;
  var statusColumnIndex = -1; // Store the column index for "Status"

  /**
   * üì° Load more rows dynamically via AJAX
   * Fetches a batch of paper records from the server and appends to the table.
   * - Updates total record count and triggers necessary post-load actions.
   * - If `is_fetchall` is true, recursively loads all pages.
   * - Re-applies filters and sorting after new rows are added.
   */
  function loadMoreRows() {
    $.ajax({
      url: ajaxmeta.ajax_url,
      type: 'GET',
      data: {
        action: 'load_paperlist',
        batch: batch,
        conf: ajaxmeta.conf,
        year: ajaxmeta.year,
        mode: ajaxmeta.mode,
        track: ajaxmeta.track,
      },
      success: function (data) {
        if (data == '0') {
          // ‚úÖ All data fetched ‚Äî hide the button
          $('#btn_fetchall').hide();
          return;
        }

        if (data.length > 0) {
          container.append(data);
          n_records += (data.match(/<tr>/g) || []).length;

          // üìå Cache numeric/text value once per cell for fast sort
          $('#paperlist tbody tr').each(function () {
            $(this).find('td').each(function () {
              $(this).attr('data-val', $(this).text().trim());
            });
          });

          $('#n_records').html(n_records);
          batch++;
          cacheStatusData();
          attachHoverHighlighting(); // ‚¨Ö Ensure this is here

          // üîÑ Apply metrics mode to new rows
          if ($('#metrics_switch').length) {
            $('#metrics_switch').trigger('change');
          }

          setTimeout(autotoggleEmptyColumns, 100); // Delay to ensure all rows are appended

        }

        if (is_fetchall) {
          loadMoreRows();
        }

        applyFilters(); // Apply filters after new rows are loaded

        // Reapply sort after loading new rows
        if (currentSortColumn !== null) {
          sortTable(currentSortColumn, currentSortAscending);
        }
      },
      error: function(xhr, status, error) {
        debugger;
          console.error('AJAX Error:', status, error);
          console.log('Response Text:', xhr.responseText);
      }
    });
  }

  /**
   * üîç Find "Status" column index dynamically
   * - Searches table headers to determine the column index of the "Status" field.
   * - Ensures compatibility even if table column order changes.
   */
  function findStatusColumnIndex() {
    statusColumnIndex = -1; // Reset before searching
    $('#paperlist thead th').each(function (index) {
      if ($(this).text().trim().toLowerCase() === "status") {
        statusColumnIndex = index;
        return false; // Stop loop once found
      }
    });
  }

  // üîÑ Find the column index on page load
  findStatusColumnIndex();

  /**
   * üè∑Ô∏è Cache paper status values in DOM
   * - Extracts status text (e.g., "withdrawn", "rejected") from each row.
   * - Stores it using jQuery `.data('status')` for faster access during filtering.
   * - Ensures repeated DOM access is minimized.
   */
  function cacheStatusData() {
    if (statusColumnIndex === -1) {
      findStatusColumnIndex(); // üîÑ Auto-find column index if not set
    }

    if (statusColumnIndex !== -1) { // Ensure "Status" column exists before proceeding
      $('#paperlist tbody tr').each(function () {
        var statusText = $(this).find('td').eq(statusColumnIndex).text().toLowerCase();
        $(this).data('status', statusText);
      });
    }
  }

  // üé¨ Initial load
  loadMoreRows();

  // when scroll to the buttom, load more
  // $(window).scroll(function () {
  //     if ($(window).scrollTop() + $(window).height() == $(document).height()) {
  //         loadMoreRows();
  //     }
  // }); // disable due to the filter could cause to the bottom of the page


  // üéØ Button: Load all records at once
  $('#btn_fetchall').click(function () {
    is_fetchall = true;
    $(this).prop('disabled', true).text('Loading...');
    loadMoreRows();  // Trigger fetch loop
  });

  // üö´ Button: Toggle rejection filter
  $('#btn_hide_reject').click(function () {
    is_hide_reject = !is_hide_reject;
    applyFilters();
  });

  /**
   * üîç Apply all active filters (column inputs + reject toggle)
   * - Loops through all rows to determine visibility based on input values.
   * - Combines rejection toggle and column input filtering.
   * - Uses `requestAnimationFrame()` for smooth UI updates.
   * - Updates visible row counts and per-column match statistics.
   */
  function applyFilters() {
    cancelAnimationFrame(filterTimeout);
    filterTimeout = requestAnimationFrame(() => {
      const filterValues = [];
      $('.filter-row input').each(function (i) {
        filterValues[i] = $(this).val().toLowerCase();
      });

      hiddenCount = 0;
      let visibleRows = 0;
      let n_index_columns = 2;

      $('#paperlist tbody tr').each(function () {
        const row = $(this);
        const cells = row.find('td');
        let showRow = true;

        for (let i = 0; i < filterValues.length; i++) {
          if (!filterValues[i]) continue;
          const cellText = cells.eq(i + n_index_columns).text().toLowerCase();
          if (!cellText.includes(filterValues[i])) {
            showRow = false;
            break;
          }
        }

        var isRejected = row.data('status').includes('withdraw') || row.data('status').includes('reject');

        if (is_hide_reject && isRejected) {
          row.css('display', 'none');
          hiddenCount++;
        } else {
          row.css('display', showRow ? '' : 'none');
          if (showRow) visibleRows++;
        }
      });

      updateHiddenCount();
      updateOverallMatchCount(visibleRows);

      // ‚úÖ Column counts now consider hidden rejected rows properly
      $('.filter-row input').each(function (i) {
        const count = singleColumnMatchCount(i + n_index_columns, filterValues[i]); // +2 to skip index and row index column
        $(this).closest('th').find('.column-match-count').text(`#: ${count}`);
      });

      autotoggleEmptyColumns();
    });
  }

  /**
 * üî¢ Update UI count of hidden (rejected/withdrawn) papers
 * - Displays total number of hidden rows.
 * - Updates toggle button label accordingly.
 */
  function updateHiddenCount() {
    $('.column-match-count.status').text(`Hidden: ${hiddenCount}`);
    $('#btn_hide_reject').text(is_hide_reject ? `Show Rejected (Hidden: ${hiddenCount})` : "Hide Rejected");
  }

  /**
 * üî¢ Display how many rows match current filters
 * - Updates summary label showing number of visible rows vs. total.
 */
  function updateOverallMatchCount(visibleRows) {
    const totalRows = $('#paperlist tbody tr').length;
    $('#filter-match-count').text(`All Filter Matches: ${visibleRows} / ${totalRows}`);
  }

  /**
   * üìä Count matches for a specific column
   * - Returns the number of visible rows that match `filterText` in column `colIndex`.
   * - Automatically excludes rejected/withdrawn rows if toggle is active.
   */
  function singleColumnMatchCount(colIndex, filterText) {
    const allRows = $('#paperlist tbody tr');

    let count = 0;
    allRows.each(function () {
      const row = $(this);
      const isRejected = row.data('status').includes('withdraw') || row.data('status').includes('reject');

      if (is_hide_reject && isRejected) {
        return; // Skip hidden rejected rows
      }

      const cellText = row.find('td').eq(colIndex).text().toLowerCase();
      if (!filterText || cellText.includes(filterText)) {
        count++;
      }
    });

    return count;
  }

  /**
   * ‚è≥ Generic debounce wrapper
   * - Ensures a function (e.g., `applyFilters`) only runs after a delay.
   * - Prevents over-triggering during rapid input events.
   */
  function debounce(func, delay) {
    return function () {
      clearTimeout(filterTimeout);
      filterTimeout = setTimeout(func, delay);
    };
  }

  // ‚å®Ô∏è Attach event listeners for filtering (with 100ms debounce)
  $('#paperlist thead').on('keyup change', '.filter-row input', debounce(applyFilters, 100));

  /******************************************************************
 * üé® Country-aware Highlighting
 * ----------------------------------------------------------------
 *  ‚Ä¢ author/affiliation/country cells share the same highlight
 *    colour chosen from their *first* country value
 *  ‚Ä¢ colours come from a user-supplied map (china ‚ûú red, us ‚ûú blue)
 *    ‚Äì any country not in the map gets an automatic pastel colour
 ******************************************************************/

  // 1Ô∏è‚É£  Custom palette for specific countries
  const COUNTRY_COLOR_MAP = {
    'china': '#ff4d4f',  // red
    'united states': '#4d79ff',
    'us': '#4d79ff',
    'usa': '#4d79ff'
  };
  const HIGHLIGHT_ALPHA = 0.8;   // global opacity (0‚Äì1)

  /**
 * üé® Generate a consistent pastel color for any country name
 * - Hashes the string to generate a hue value.
 * - Returns HSLA color string with preset saturation/lightness.
 */
  function autoColor(name) {
    let hash = 0;
    for (let i = 0; i < name.length; i++)
      hash = name.charCodeAt(i) + ((hash << 5) - hash);
    const hue = Math.abs(hash) % 360;
    return `hsla(${hue},70%,85%,${HIGHLIGHT_ALPHA})`;
  }

  /**
 * üé® Convert hex color string to RGBA with optional opacity
 * - Supports 3-digit and 6-digit hex formats.
 * - Used for COUNTRY_COLOR_MAP values.
 */
  function hexToRgba(hex, alpha = HIGHLIGHT_ALPHA) {
    hex = hex.replace('#', '');
    if (hex.length === 3) hex = hex.split('').map(c => c + c).join('');
    const int = parseInt(hex, 16);
    const r = (int >> 16) & 255,
      g = (int >> 8) & 255,
      b = int & 255;
    return `rgba(${r},${g},${b},${alpha})`;
  }

  /**
   * üåê Resolve country to highlight color
   * - Uses predefined COUNTRY_COLOR_MAP if available.
   * - Falls back to auto-generated pastel color.
   */
  function countryToColor(country) {
    const key = (country || '').toLowerCase().trim();
    const base = COUNTRY_COLOR_MAP[key];
    return base ? hexToRgba(base) : autoColor(key);
  }

  /**
 * ‚ú® Attach hover highlight logic for author/affiliation/country
 * - Adds event listeners to highlight related table cells based on shared attributes.
 * - Uses country-based color mapping for consistent highlighting.
 * - Applies background color and transition effect.
 */
  function attachHoverHighlighting() {

    function colourize($el, colour, base) {
      $el.css({
        'background-color': colour,
        // 'border': `1px solid ${base}`,   // inner border for definition
        'transition': 'background-color 0.12s'
      }).attr('data-coloured', '1');
    }

    function clearHighlights($row) {
      $row.find('[data-coloured="1"]').removeAttr('style data-coloured');
    }

    function matchAny($row, selector, dataKey, values, colour, base) {
      values.forEach(val => {
        $row.find(`${selector}[data-${dataKey}*="${val}"]`).each(function () {
          const targetVals = (`${$(this).data(dataKey)}`).split('+');
          if (targetVals.includes(val)) colourize($(this), colour, base);
        });
      });
    }

    /* ---------- EVENT BINDINGS ---------- */
    $(document).on('mouseenter', '.author-link', function () {
      const $row = $(this).closest('tr');
      const affs = (`${$(this).data('aff')}`).split('+');
      const countries = (`${$(this).data('country')}`).split('+');
      const base = COUNTRY_COLOR_MAP[(countries[0] || '').toLowerCase()] || autoColor(countries[0] || '');
      const fill = countryToColor(countries[0] || '');

      matchAny($row, '.aff-link', 'aff', affs, fill, base);
      matchAny($row, '.country-link', 'index', countries, fill, base);
      colourize($(this), fill, base);
    }).on('mouseleave', '.author-link', function () {
      clearHighlights($(this).closest('tr'));
    });

    $(document).on('mouseenter', '.aff-link', function () {
      const $row = $(this).closest('tr');
      const affs = (`${$(this).data('aff')}`).split('+');
      const countries = (`${$(this).data('country')}`).split('+');
      const base = COUNTRY_COLOR_MAP[(countries[0] || '').toLowerCase()] || autoColor(countries[0] || '');
      const fill = countryToColor(countries[0] || '');

      matchAny($row, '.author-link', 'aff', affs, fill, base);
      matchAny($row, '.country-link', 'index', countries, fill, base);
      colourize($(this), fill, base);
    }).on('mouseleave', '.aff-link', function () {
      clearHighlights($(this).closest('tr'));
    });

    $(document).on('mouseenter', '.country-link', function () {
      const $row = $(this).closest('tr');
      const idx = `${$(this).data('index')}`;
      const name = $(this).text().trim();
      const base = COUNTRY_COLOR_MAP[name.toLowerCase()] || autoColor(name);
      const fill = countryToColor(name);

      matchAny($row, '.author-link', 'country', [idx], fill, base);
      matchAny($row, '.aff-link', 'country', [idx], fill, base);
      colourize($(this), fill, base);
    }).on('mouseleave', '.country-link', function () {
      clearHighlights($(this).closest('tr'));
    });
  }

  // üîÑ  Re-attach after every AJAX batch

  $('body').append('<div id="author-popup" style="position:absolute;display:none;padding:6px 10px;background:#fff;border:1px solid #ccc;border-radius:6px;font-size:13px;z-index:10000;box-shadow:2px 2px 5px rgba(0,0,0,0.1);"></div>');

  // Add the floating profile popup div (only once)
  if (!$('#author-popup').length) {
    $('body').append(`
      <div id="author-popup" style="
        position:absolute;
        display:none;
        padding:10px 14px;
        background:#fefefe;
        border:1px solid #bbb;
        border-radius:8px;
        font-size:13px;
        z-index:10000;
        box-shadow:0 4px 10px rgba(0,0,0,0.2);
        transition: opacity 0.2s ease;
        line-height:1.6;
      "></div>
    `);
  }

  let hidePopupTimeout = null;

  // Hover on author span
  $(document).on('mouseenter', '.author-link', function (e) {
    clearTimeout(hidePopupTimeout);

    const gs = $(this).data('gs');
    const hp = $(this).data('hp');
    const dblp = $(this).data('dblp');
    const or = $(this).data('or');
    const name = $(this).text().trim();

    // ‚úÖ Skip popup if all links are missing
    if (!gs && !hp && !dblp && !or) return;

    let content = `
      <div style="font-weight:bold; font-size:14px; margin-bottom:6px;">${name}</div>
      <div style="margin-top:4px;">
        ${gs ? `<a href="${gs}" target="_blank" style="color:#0645ad;text-decoration:none;display:block;margin-bottom:4px;">Google Scholar</a>` : ''}
        ${hp ? `<a href="${hp}" target="_blank" style="color:#0645ad;text-decoration:none;display:block;">Homepage</a>` : ''}
        ${dblp ? `<a href="${dblp}" target="_blank" style="color:#0645ad;text-decoration:none;display:block;margin-top:4px;">DBLP</a>` : ''}
        ${or ? `<a href="${or}" target="_blank" style="color:#0645ad;text-decoration:none;display:block;margin-top:4px;">OpenReview</a>` : ''}
      </div>
    `;

    $('#author-popup')
      .html(content)
      .css({
        top: e.pageY + 12 + 'px',
        left: e.pageX - 12 + 'px',
        display: 'block',
        opacity: 1
      });
  }).on('mousemove', '.author-link', function (e) {
    $('#author-popup').css({
      top: e.pageY + 12 + 'px',
      left: e.pageX - 12 + 'px'
    });
  }).on('mouseleave', '.author-link', function () {
    hidePopupTimeout = setTimeout(() => {
      $('#author-popup').fadeOut(150);
    }, 400);
  });

  // Prevent flicker when hovering into popup
  $(document).on('mouseenter', '#author-popup', function () {
    clearTimeout(hidePopupTimeout);
  }).on('mouseleave', '#author-popup', function () {
    $('#author-popup').fadeOut(50);
  });


  $('#aff_switch').on('change', function () {
    const mode = $(this).val();
    $('.aff-link').each(function () {
      const dep = $(this).data('dep');
      const campus = $(this).data('campus');
      const norm = $(this).data('norm');
      const abbr = $(this).data('abbr');
      const url = $(this).data('url');

      let text = norm;
      if (mode === 'dep') {
        if (dep || campus) {
          text = `${dep ? `<span style="color:#555;font-style:italic;">${dep}</span>, ` : ''}` +
            `${campus ? `<span style="color:#999;">${campus}</span>, ` : ''}` +
            norm;
        }
      } else if (mode === 'abbr') {
        text = abbr || norm;
      }

      const link = url ? `<a href="${url}" target="_blank">${text}</a>` : text;
      $(this).html(link);
    });
  });

  $('#metrics_switch').on('change', function () {
    const mode = $(this).val();
    $('.metrics-cell').each(function () {
      const $cell = $(this);
      if (mode === 'gs' || mode === 'rating_avg' || mode === 'rating_str') {
        const html = $cell.data(mode);
        $cell.html(html ?? '');
      } else {
        const val = $cell.data(mode);
        $cell.text(val ?? '');
      }
    });

  });

  $('#rating_avg_switch').on('change', function () {
    const mode = $(this).val();
    $('.rating-cell').each(function () {
      const $cell = $(this);
      if (mode === 'all') {
        const html = $cell.attr('data-all');
        $cell.html(html ?? '');
      } else {
        const val = $cell.data(mode);
        $cell.text(val ?? '');
      }
    });
  });
  
  $('#confidence_avg_switch').on('change', function () {
    const mode = $(this).val();
    $('.confidence-cell').each(function () {
      const $cell = $(this);
      if (mode === 'all') {
        const html = $cell.attr('data-all');
        $cell.html(html ?? '');
      } else {
        const val = $cell.data(mode);
        $cell.text(val ?? '');
      }
    });
  });
  

  let currentSortColumn = null;
  let currentSortAscending = true;

  /**
 * üìä Sort table rows by selected column
 * - Handles both numeric and textual sorting.
 * - Updates row numbering in first column.
 * - Maintains sort state globally (ascending/descending).
 * - Calls `autotoggleEmptyColumns()` after reordering.
 */
  function sortTable(colIndex, ascending) {
    const tbody = document.querySelector('#paperlist tbody');
    const rows = Array.from(tbody.rows);          // live HTMLCollection ‚Üí real array

    /* ---- 1Ô∏è‚É£  read-once, work on JS objects only ----------------------- */
    const numeric = rows.every(r => {
      // const txt = r.cells[colIndex].dataset.val ?? r.cells[colIndex].textContent.trim();
      const txt = r.cells[colIndex].textContent.trim();
      return txt === '' || !isNaN(+txt);
    });

    rows.sort((a, b) => {
      // const A = a.cells[colIndex].dataset.val ?? a.cells[colIndex].textContent;
      // const B = b.cells[colIndex].dataset.val ?? b.cells[colIndex].textContent;
      const A = a.cells[colIndex].textContent;
      const B = b.cells[colIndex].textContent;

      return numeric
        ? (ascending ? +A - +B : +B - +A)
        : (ascending ? A.localeCompare(B) : B.localeCompare(A));
    });

    /* ---- 2Ô∏è‚É£  write-back in one go (no re-flows in the loop) ----------- */
    // Determine if we're back in original order (for R# hiding)
    let allMatchOriginal = true;
    rows.forEach((row, i) => {
      const originalIndex = parseInt(row.cells[1].textContent.trim()); // original #
      const newIndex = i + 1;
      if (originalIndex !== newIndex) allMatchOriginal = false;
      // row.cells[0].textContent = newIndex; // update R#
      row.cells[0].innerHTML = '<small>' + newIndex + '</small>'; // update R# with small font
    });

    // Reorder rows in DOM
    const frag = document.createDocumentFragment();
    rows.forEach(row => frag.appendChild(row));
    tbody.appendChild(frag);

    // Hide index column if not sorted
    if (allMatchOriginal) {
      rows.forEach(row => row.cells[0].innerHTML = '');
    }

    autotoggleEmptyColumns(); // Recheck empty columns after sorting
  }

  $(document).on('click', '.sort-btn', function () {
    const colIndex = parseInt($(this).data('col'));

    // Toggle and store global state
    if (currentSortColumn === colIndex) {
      currentSortAscending = !currentSortAscending;
    } else {
      currentSortColumn = colIndex;
      currentSortAscending = true;
    }

    sortTable(colIndex, currentSortAscending);

    // Update all buttons
    $('.sort-btn').each(function () {
      const idx = $(this).data('col');
      const isCurrent = idx === currentSortColumn;
      $(this).text(isCurrent ? (currentSortAscending ? '‚¨ç A-Z' : '‚¨ç Z-A') : '‚¨ç A-Z');
    });
  });

  /**
 * üßΩ Automatically hide empty columns
 * - Checks if each column contains only empty cells.
 * - If so, hides both `<th>` and `<td>` elements for that column.
 * - Supports merged headers via `colspan`.
 */
  function autotoggleEmptyColumns() {
    const $table = $('#paperlist');
    const $tbodyRows = $table.find('tbody tr');
    const numCols = $tbodyRows.first().find('td').length;

    const emptyCols = new Array(numCols).fill(true);

    // 1Ô∏è‚É£ Detect truly empty columns
    $tbodyRows.each(function () {
      $(this).find('td').each(function (i) {
        if ($(this).text().trim() !== '') {
          emptyCols[i] = false;
        }
      });
    });

    // 2Ô∏è‚É£ Hide <th> and <td> for empty columns, mark as .auto-hidden
    $table.find('thead tr').each(function () {
      let colIdx = 0;
      $(this).children('th').each(function () {
        const colspan = parseInt($(this).attr('colspan')) || 1;
        const coversEmpty = emptyCols.slice(colIdx, colIdx + colspan).every(v => v);

        if (coversEmpty) {
          $(this).addClass('auto-hidden').hide();
        } else {
          $(this).removeClass('auto-hidden').show();
        }

        colIdx += colspan;
      });
    });

    $tbodyRows.each(function () {
      $(this).find('td').each(function (i) {
        if (emptyCols[i]) {
          $(this).addClass('auto-hidden').hide();
        } else {
          $(this).removeClass('auto-hidden').show();
        }
      });
    });
  }

});

```
